# Working Knowledge Block Reward Audit

Generated by `tools/generate-working-knowledge-balance.ps1`. This report evaluates every generated research catalog block against the current schematic work reward table. It does not change tuning.

## Summary

- Cataloged block rows: 1411
- Unresolved catalog rows: 0
- Rows marked `review`: 3
- Rows marked `expected`: 12
- `Reward` is the medium-difficulty full-grind work reward before the research curve is applied.
- `Repeated Grinds` estimates how many full grinds of that same block would unlock the schematic at medium settings with the current research curve.
- `Grid Ratio` compares the block against its expected family anchor: `1.00` for the large-grid anchor block, `1.00` for the small-grid anchor block after the intended 0.25 small-grid factor.
